   /* &lt;![CDATA[ */
$(document).ready(function() {
	$("#writeReviewIframe").load(function() {
		$("#writeReviewIframe").attr("height", $("#writeReviewIframe").contents().get(0).body.scrollHeight - 125);
	});
	interv = setInterval('assignReviewsClickEvents()', 500);
});
var flag = false;
var interv = null;
var pr_locale = "en_US";
var pr_zip_location = "http://cdn.dick-blick.com/pwrroot";
var pr_style_sheet = "http://www.dickblick.com/styles/pr_override_styles.css?v=5";
var prPageId = "259";

function assignReviewsClickEvents() {
	if ($("div.pr-snippet-write-review a.pr-snippet-link") != undefined &amp;&amp; $("div.pr-snapshot-footer a.pr-write-review-link") != undefined &amp;&amp; $("div.pr-snippet-read-reviews a.pr-snippet-link") != undefined) {
		$("div.pr-snippet-write-first-review a.pr-snippet-link, div.pr-snippet-write-review a.pr-snippet-link, div.pr-snapshot-footer a.pr-write-review-link").click(function() {
			showReviewsTab('writereviews', 'readreviews');
		});
		$("div.pr-snippet-read-reviews a.pr-snippet-link").click(function() {
			showReviewsTab('readreviews', 'writereviews');
		});
		clearInterval(interv);
	}
}

function showReviewsTab() {
	$("#producttab_reviews").trigger("click");
	$("#" + arguments[0]).show();
	$("#" + arguments[1]).hide();
	if (arguments[0] == "writereviews" &amp;&amp; flag == false) {
		$("#writeReviewIframe").attr("src", "/Code/PageTemplates/reviews.aspx?pageid=259&amp;vid=&amp;source=0");
		flag = true;
	}
}
/* ]]&gt; */
  </script>

  </script>
  <script type="text/javascript">
   $(document).ready(function () {
            $('.skuquantity').find('input:text').each(function () {
                $("&lt;input type='number' class='skuquantitybox' value='0' size='2' maxlength='3' /&gt;").attr({ name: this.name }).insertBefore(this);
            }).remove();

            $('.skuquantitybox').each(function () {
                var default_value = this.value;
                $(this).focus(function () {
                    if (this.value == default_value) {
                        this.value = '';
                    }
                });
                $(this).blur(function () {
                    if (this.value == '') {
                        this.value = default_value;
                    }
                });
            });
        });
  </script>

        <div class="title" id="producttitle">
         <table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="table-layout: auto;">
          <tr>
           <td align="left" id="ctl00_ContentPlaceHolder1_titlecell" valign="top" width="100%">
            <a href="/customerservice/returns/">
             <img alt="100% Satisfaction Guaranteed" id="guaranteed" src="http://cdn.dick-blick.com/images/adbanner/100-Satisfaction-Banner-210x50.jpg"/>
            </a>
            <h1>
             Rembrandt Artists' Oil Colors
            </h1>
           </td>
          </tr>
         </table>
        </div>

        <div class="info" id="maintab">
         <table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" id="maintabinfo" width="100%">
          <tr>
           <td valign="top" width="50%">
            <div class="description" id="descriptionblock">
             <div class="copy" id="copyblock">
              <p class="body">
               Rembrandt Artists' Oil Colors are manufactured to exacting professional quality standards in Apeldoorn, Holland. They respond to the brush with a buttery feel, and have a noticeable brilliance and color intensity rarely seen anywhere in the world.
              </p>
              <p class="body">
               Rembrandt Oils are highly durable and are produced with the highest color strength possible, using valuable, costly, pure pigments. The pigments are ground to extreme fineness in a binder consisting of the purest linseed or safflower seed oil, resulting in an oil paint whose texture is exceptionally smooth, creamy, and even.
              </p>
             </div>
             <div id="notesblock">
              <div class="notes">
               <p>
                <strong>
                 Color Chart note
                </strong>
                 Use this color chart as an approximation of the real color. If exact color matching is necessary, use actual samples of the materials.
               </p>
               <p>
                <strong>
                 Caution
                </strong>
                 Follow safety instructions carefully. Shipping restrictions apply to hazardous materials.
               </p>
              </div>
             </div>
             <div class="specs" id="specsblock" style="display: none;">
              <p class="body">
              </p>
              <table border="1" cellpadding="1" cellspacing="1" summary="" width="200">
               <tbody>
                <tr>
                 <td>
                  Tube
                 </td>
                 <td>
                  40 ml
                 </td>
                 <td>
                  1.4 oz
                 </td>
                </tr>
                <tr>
                 <td>
                  Tube
                 </td>
                 <td>
                  150 ml
                 </td>
                 <td>
                  5.1 oz
                 </td>
                </tr>
               </tbody>
              </table>
              <p class="body">
               All Rembrandt Artist's Oil Colors are AP non-toxic, except for the following colors which bear the ACMI Caution Label.
              </p>
              <ul>
               <li>
                Aureoline
               </li>
               <li>
                Cadmium Orange
               </li>
               <li>
                Cadmium Red Medium
               </li>
               <li>
                Cadmium Red Deep
               </li>
               <li>
                Cadmium Red Light
               </li>
               <li>
                Cadmium Red Purple
               </li>
               <li>
                Cadmium Yellow Deep
               </li>
               <li>
                Cadmium Yellow Lemon
               </li>
               <li>
                Cadmium Yellow Light
               </li>
               <li>
                Cadmium Yellow Medium
               </li>
               <li>
                Cerulean Blue
               </li>
               <li>
                Chromium Oxide Green
               </li>
               <li>
                Cobalt Blue Deep
               </li>
               <li>
                Cobalt Blue Light
               </li>
               <li>
                Cobalt Green
               </li>
               <li>
                Cobalt Turquoise Blue
               </li>
               <li>
                Cobalt Turquoise Green
               </li>
               <li>
                Cobalt Violet
               </li>
               <li>
                Kings Blue
               </li>
              </ul>
              <p align="center" class="corporate">
              </p>

               <div class="pr-review-text">
                <p class="pr-comments-header">
                 Comments about
                 <em>
                  <span class="pr-product-name">
                   Rembrandt Artists' Oil Colors
                  </span>
                 </em>
                 :
                </p>
                <p class="pr-comments">
                 Reading Richard Schmidt's book Everything I Know about Painting he talked about they colors and brands of oil paint he uses. He used several brands but especially recommended Rembrandts Transparent Red Oxide and Viridian. I have tried them and now rarely use burnt sienna. They quality of Rembrandt's oil are extraordinary.
                </p>
               </div>

           <h1 style="margin: 10px 0px 20px 0px;">
            Help with Ordering
           </h1>
           <div style="text-align: left;">
            <p style="margin: 10px;">
             <strong>
              Add to Cart
             </strong>
              find the materials you want to purchase in the price table. 
			Enter quantities and press Add to Cart. Materials that you select are not added to your cart until you press Add to Cart.
            </p>
            <p style="margin: 10px;">
             <strong>
              Shopping Cart
             </strong>
              to view your cart, or to check out, click on Shopping Cart.
			(A shopping cart icon is also located in the navigation bar at the top of the page.)
            </p>
            <p style="margin: 10px;">
             <strong>
              Sortable Columns
             </strong>
              click on the column heading to sort the table.  
			For example, click on Color to sort by the color names or click on Price to sort by price (where available).
            </p>
            <p style="margin: 10px;">
             <strong>
              Expected Date
             </strong>
              if we are out of stock, the date given underneath is the date that the 
			backordered item is expected to arrive at Dick Blick's central Illinois warehouse. To estimate when the item 
			will be delivered to your door, add up to 10 business days to the Expected Date, 
			depending on your location and method of shipment.
            </p>
            <p style="margin: 10px;">
             <strong>
              Backorders
             </strong>
              if you order an item that we stock in our warehouse, and we are out of stock, 
			we backorder that item for you automatically.
            </p>
           </div>
           <p style="text-align: center; font-size: x-small; margin: 8% auto 3px auto; padding: 0;">
            <strong>
             Hint
            </strong>
             click anywhere in this window to close
           </p>

           /*test value for non negative integer*/
	var $intpositiveval = function(value) {
		return /^\d+$/.test(value) &amp;&amp; parseInt(value) &gt; 0;
	};

	$(document).ready(function() {
		$("#addToCartForm").append("&lt;input type=\"hidden\" id=\"listinfo\" name=\"listinfo\" value=\"\" /&gt;");
		$("#addToCartForm").append("&lt;input type=\"hidden\" id=\"listname\" name=\"listname\" value=\"\" /&gt;");
		
		$("input.btn_add").click(function() {
			if ($("#listNameFld").val() != "") {
				var $validQuantities = true;
				$("input.skuquantitybox[value != '0'], input.skuquantityboxWarn[value != '0']").each(function() {
					if (!$intpositiveval($(this).val())) {
						$validQuantities = false;
						return;
					}
				});
				if ($("input.skuquantitybox[value != '0'], input.skuquantityboxWarn[value != '0']").size() &gt; 0 &amp;&amp; $validQuantities) {
				$("#listinfo").val($("#listNameFld").val());

					//alert($('select option:selected').text());
					//return false;
					$('#listname').val($('select option:selected').text());

					// toggle post action iif ARA...
					if ($('#listNameFld').val().substring(0, 1) == '2') {
						// create new list...
						if ($('#listNameFld').val() == '2_0') {
							$("#addToCartForm").attr({ action: 'http://www.dickblick.com/ara/lists/create' });
						}
						// adding to existing...
						else {
							var listID = $('#listNameFld').val().split('_')[1];
							var listGUID = $('#listNameFld').val().split('_')[2];
							//alert('listGUID = ' + listGUID);

							var quantities = '';
							var skus = '';
							$("input.skuquantitybox[value != '0'], input.skuquantityboxWarn[value != '0']").each(function() {
								quantities += $(this).val() + ',';
								skus += $(this).attr('id').replace('_qtybox', '') + ',';
							});

							//alert('quantities = ' + quantities.slice(0, -1) + ' &amp; skus = ' + skus.slice(0, -1));
							//return false;
							//$("#addToCartForm").attr({ action: 'http://www.dickblick.com/ara/Services/Lists.svc/add-item/' });
							

				$("#addToCartForm").attr({ action: '/lists/additems/' });
						}
					}
					else {
						$("#addToCartForm").attr({ action: '/lists/additems/' });
					}
					
				$("#addToCartForm").submit();
				}
				else {
					$("#skuactions").children("div.msg_error").children("p").text("Please enter a valid quantity.");
					$("#skuactions").children("div.msg_error").show();
				}
			}
			else {
				$("#skuactions").children("div.msg_error").children("p").text("Please select one of your Lists or create a new List.");
			   $("#skuactions").children("div.msg_error").show();
			}
			return false;
		});
		$("input.btn_addToCart").click(function() {
			var $validQuantities = true;
			$("input.skuquantitybox[value != '0'], input.skuquantityboxWarn[value != '0']").each(function() {
				if (!$intpositiveval($(this).val())) {
					$validQuantities = false;
					return;
				}
			});
			if ($("input.skuquantitybox[value != '0'], input.skuquantityboxWarn[value != '0']").size() &gt; 0 &amp;&amp; $validQuantities) {

				try {
				var productsLine = "";
				var eventsLine = "scAdd";
				$("input.skuquantitybox[value != '0'], input.skuquantityboxWarn[value != '0']").each(function () {
						var productSku = $(this).attr("id").replace("_qtybox", "");
						if (/^\d{5}-\d{4}$/.test(productSku)) {
							productsLine = productsLine + ";" + productSku + ",";
						}
						else {
							/* handles sku page */
							productsLine = productsLine + ";" + $(this).parents("td").children().first().val() + ",";
						}
				});
				if (productsLine.length &gt; 0) {
					productsLine = productsLine.substr(0, productsLine.length - 1);
                        
                        //Custom DW Variables to import GA information
                        GADWCustomVariables();

						/* track Cart Add Items event in GA */
						var eventCategory = "Cart";
						var eventAction = "Add Items" + " (Open Cart)";
						var eventLabel = '(P8MGA4D60JP78MF3VM9QP1WFCGBV3WR3) ' + window.location.pathname + ' (' + productsLine.replace(/;/g, "") + ')';
                        pageTracker._trackEvent(eventCategory, eventAction, eventLabel); 

						/* setting Omniture SiteCatalyst vars */
					eventsLine = eventsLine + ",scOpen";
				    if('False' == "True"){
					    s.linkTrackVars = "products,events";
					    s.linkTrackEvents = eventsLine;
					    s.products = productsLine;
					    s.events = eventsLine;
					    s.tl(true, 'o', 'Add to Cart');
                    }
				}
				}
				catch (err) { }

				$("#addToCartForm").attr({ action: '/cart/add/' });
				$("#addToCartForm").submit();
			}
			else {
				$("#skuactions").children("div.msg_error").children("p").text("Please enter a valid quantity.");
				$("#skuactions").children("div.msg_error").show();
			}
			return false;
		});
		$("a.loginlink").click(function() {
			$("#listinfo").val("0_0");
			$("#addToCartForm").attr({ action: '/lists/additems/' });
			$("#addToCartForm").submit();
			return false;
		});
	});
          </script>

   var gaJsHost = (("https:" == document.location.protocol) ? "https://ssl." : "http://www.");

  <script type="text/javascript">
   try {
	    var pageTracker = _gat._createTracker("UA-1407916-1");
		
} catch (err) { }

	//Declaring UID Variable - DW Integration
	function s4() {
	    return Math.floor((1 + Math.random()) * 0x10000).toString(16).substring(1);
	};

	function AddCookie(name, value, expirationDays) {
	    var expirationDate = new Date();
	    expirationDate.setTime(expirationDate.getTime() + (expirationDays * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
	    document.cookie = name + "=" + value + "; expires=" + expirationDate.toGMTString() + "; path=/";
	};

	function GetCookie(name) {
	    var regEx = new RegExp(name + "=([^;]+)");
	    var cookieValue = regEx.exec(document.cookie);
	    return (cookieValue != null) ? unescape(cookieValue[1]) : null;
	};

	function GUID() {
	    // try to get the GUID from localstorage - get GUID from cart storage if a user already has a GUID 
	    var storedGUIDCookie = GetCookie("gaUID");

	    //Verify if storedGUID exists - if exists use that GUID, if not use GUID that is generated from uniqueIdentifier
	    if (storedGUIDCookie != null &amp;&amp; storedGUIDCookie != '')
	        return storedGUIDCookie;

	    //Generate random GUID and store in uniqueIdentifier
	    var uniqueIdentifier = s4() + s4() + '-' + s4() + '-' + s4() + '-' + s4() + '-' + s4() + s4() + s4();
	    AddCookie("gaUID", uniqueIdentifier, 90);

	    //Return uniqueIdentifer to allow to be accessed
	    return uniqueIdentifier;
	};

	var uniqueID = GUID();

	//Declaring ShopperId in webAnalytics.ascx.vb file - accessing it here
	var shopperId = 'P8MGA4D60JP78MF3VM9QP1WFCGBV3WR3';

//Function for custom GA DW Analytics variables (pageview level - the custom variable data only persists during the current pageview) - accessed in each GA event across db.com
var GADWCustomVariables = function () {
    //Custom Variable Identifiers used by DW Population
    pageTracker._setCustomVar(1, 'DWUniqueID', uniqueID, 3);
    pageTracker._setCustomVar(2, 'ShopperID', shopperId, 3);

    return this;
};

GADWCustomVariables();
pageTracker._trackPageview();
  </script>
